          <hr class="section-divider">
         </div>
         <div class="section-content">
          <div class="section-inner sectionLayout--insetColumn">
           <h1 name="6858" id="6858" class="graf graf--h3 graf--leading graf--title">Making Atom (even more) awesome?—?My&nbsp;Setup</h1>
           <p name="e41b" id="e41b" class="graf graf--p graf-after--h3">I spent a long time researching, trying and tweaking text editors. As a cross-platform developer and technical writer (mostly writer these days) I work with different programming languages, document formats and want an editor with particular features, but that is also easy on the eye. Ideally I wanted all the functionality I was looking for in one application, not split between 5.</p>
           <p name="e931" id="e931" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">Here’s what I was looking for:</p>
           <ul class="postList">
            <li name="d741" id="d741" class="graf graf--li graf-after--p">Good Markdown support.</li>
            <li name="2394" id="2394" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">The ability to export markdown to different formats (at least PDF and HTML).</li>
            <li name="5264" id="5264" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">A project manager.</li>
            <li name="4d0e" id="4d0e" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">Spelling and grammar checking.</li>
            <li name="a6c2" id="a6c2" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">The ability to edit code inline (in markdown) as well as in separate files and for it to be formatted and highlighted correctly.</li>
            <li name="2aa6" id="2aa6" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">An extension / plugin architecture for features I don’t even know I want yet.</li>
           </ul>
           <p name="4ee2" id="4ee2" class="graf graf--p graf-after--li">Open Source would be a bonus, but it wasn’t essential. I am happy to pay for software, but cost isn’t always an indication of quality.</p>
           <p name="7e58" id="7e58" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">I tried <a href="https://www.sublimetext.com/3" data-href="https://www.sublimetext.com/3" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Sublime</a> for a while but got bored with it and can’t even remember why. I tried <a href="http://www.barebones.com/products/bbedit/" data-href="http://www.barebones.com/products/bbedit/" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">BBEdit</a> (and TextWrangler), I liked that it was Mac-native but it lacked a lot of the features I required for the money it cost. I tried <a href="http://brackets.io/" data-href="http://brackets.io/" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Brackets</a> some time ago, and again I can’t remember what I didn’t like about it, but I moved on quickly. <a href="http://macromates.com/" data-href="http://macromates.com/" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">TextMate</a> was nearly there, but again it wasn’t worth the money, I would still need other tools.</p>
           <p name="5b8f" id="5b8f" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">Then I found <a href="http://atom.io" data-href="http://atom.io" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Atom</a> from GitHub. I wasn’t immediately convinced, versions prior to version 1 were unreliable and certain features necessary to me didn’t work well (HTML and PDF export), but something about Atom made me want to stick with it.</p>
           <p name="39fd" id="39fd" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">Atom is a text editor, so of course will work with anything text-related. However they are often primarily aimed at coders and setting things up for a more writing focused workflow takes a few steps and after months of tinkering I have arrived at a near perfect (I will regret saying that) setup for me and I wanted to share what I use, how I’ve configured it, and what it helps me do.</p>
           <p name="6ab1" id="6ab1" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">I’m considering making an Atom fork or special package file that bundles these writer specific plugins and setting together, but that’s still an idea.</p>
           <h4 name="2d6b" id="2d6b" class="graf graf--h4 graf-after--p">Making Atom Look&nbsp;Nice(r)</h4>
           <p name="7b36" id="7b36" class="graf graf--p graf-after--h4">I like light themes, and use <a href="https://atom.io/themes/one-o-eight-syntax" data-href="https://atom.io/themes/one-o-eight-syntax" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">one-o-eight-syntax</a> in <em class="markup--em markup--p-em">light</em> and <em class="markup--em markup--p-em">bright</em> variants.</p>
           <figure name="6e16" id="6e16" class="graf graf--figure graf-after--p">
            <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder is-locked" style="max-width: 700px; max-height: 198px;">

           <p name="a018" id="a018" class="graf graf--p graf-after--figure">It looks like this (plus other additions which I will cover next).</p>

           <p name="c95e" id="c95e" class="graf graf--p graf-after--figure">I used to have a couple of customisation in my <em class="markup--em markup--p-em">styles.less</em> file, but I have removed all of them now, so this is default.</p>
           <p name="2a49" id="2a49" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">I use the <a href="https://atom.io/themes/unity-ui" data-href="https://atom.io/themes/unity-ui" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Unity UI theme</a>, as I like my Mac software to look like Mac software.</p>
           <p name="2ce2" id="2ce2" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p"><a href="https://atom.io/packages/atom-html-preview" data-href="https://atom.io/packages/atom-html-preview" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Atom HTML Preview</a> is great for previewing HTML files.</p>
           <figure name="3b6c" id="3b6c" class="graf graf--figure graf--iframe graf-after--p">
            <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder is-locked">
             <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder-fill" style="padding-bottom: 75%;"></div>
             <div class="iframeContainer">
              <iframe data-width="640" data-height="480" width="640" height="480" src="/media/d6eef7fba653444b9d7cd2a788f11d27?postId=e7a89969a876" data-media-id="d6eef7fba653444b9d7cd2a788f11d27" allowfullscreen frameborder="0"></iframe>
             </div>
            </div>
           </figure>
           <p name="b4cc" id="b4cc" class="graf graf--p graf-after--figure">I have increasingly poor eyesight, and I find <a href="https://atom.io/packages/highlight-line" data-href="https://atom.io/packages/highlight-line" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Highlight Line</a> helpful for identifying where I am in a document. It’s also customisable to suit your needs.</p>
           <figure name="9617" id="9617" class="graf graf--figure graf-after--p">
            <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder is-locked" style="max-width: 700px; max-height: 93px;">
             <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder-fill" style="padding-bottom: 13.200000000000001%;"></div>
             <img class="graf-image" data-image-id="1*VCHgcWBucsD5PAyNTi2kQQ.png" data-width="734" data-height="97" data-action="zoom" data-action-value="1*VCHgcWBucsD5PAyNTi2kQQ.png" src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/max/1600/1*VCHgcWBucsD5PAyNTi2kQQ.png">
            </div>
           </figure>
           <p name="7b53" id="7b53" class="graf graf--p graf-after--figure"><a href="https://atom.io/packages/atom-beautify" data-href="https://atom.io/packages/atom-beautify" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Atom Beautify</a> is a comprehensive package that formats your code (and text), and lets you configure what ‘beautifier’ to use for what supported language.</p>
           <figure name="1a63" id="1a63" class="graf graf--figure graf-after--p">
            <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder is-locked" style="max-width: 700px; max-height: 370px;">

              <img src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/freeze/max/60/1*KblVpWuj0qxxnRNkWbfESw.png?q=20" crossorigin="anonymous" class="progressiveMedia-thumbnail js-progressiveMedia-thumbnail">
              <canvas class="progressiveMedia-canvas js-progressiveMedia-canvas"></canvas>
              <img class="progressiveMedia-image js-progressiveMedia-image" data-src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/max/1600/1*KblVpWuj0qxxnRNkWbfESw.png">

              </noscript>
             </div>
            </div>
           </figure>
           <p name="11cf" id="11cf" class="graf graf--p graf-after--figure">And then triggering the command will tidy your code/text for you.</p>
           <figure name="cd71" id="cd71" class="graf graf--figure graf--iframe graf-after--p">
            <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder is-locked">
             <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder-fill" style="padding-bottom: 56.2%;"></div>
             <div class="iframeContainer">

             </div>
            </div>
           </figure>
           <p name="823b" id="823b" class="graf graf--p graf-after--figure">In conjunction with Atom Beautify I use the <a href="https://atom.io/packages/tidy-markdown" data-href="https://atom.io/packages/tidy-markdown" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Tidy Markdown</a> package that I find does a better job than the inbuilt package.</p>
           <p name="2e09" id="2e09" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">Personally I am not a big fan of the 80 character per line limit, as you can achieve this with layout and flow accordingly. But if you work with projects who insist on it, you can use <a href="https://atom.io/packages/line-length-break" data-href="https://atom.io/packages/line-length-break" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Break Line Length</a> to force line breaks at a defined length before submitting your work.</p>
           <figure name="33ca" id="33ca" class="graf graf--figure graf--iframe graf-after--p">
            <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder is-locked">
             <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder-fill" style="padding-bottom: 75%;"></div>
             <div class="iframeContainer">
              <iframe data-width="640" data-height="480" width="640" height="480" src="/media/783cc8932bf6969ba8d6dea13e5821da?postId=e7a89969a876" data-media-id="783cc8932bf6969ba8d6dea13e5821da" allowfullscreen frameborder="0"></iframe>
             </div>
            </div>
           </figure>
           <p name="c72b" id="c72b" class="graf graf--p graf-after--figure"><a href="https://atom.io/packages/multi-wrap-guide" data-href="https://atom.io/packages/multi-wrap-guide" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Multi wrap guide</a> lets you set wrap guides at configurable positions, it should also work with the package above to break text at these positions.</p>
           <p name="2dee" id="2dee" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p"><a href="https://atom.io/packages/pigments" data-href="https://atom.io/packages/pigments" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Pigments</a> shows colour values inline, simple but nice ?.</p>
           <h4 name="ab46" id="ab46" class="graf graf--h4 graf-after--p">Language Formatters, Linters and&nbsp;Snippets</h4>
           <p name="353e" id="353e" class="graf graf--p graf-after--h4">Many of these will be self-explanatory (and I wont include screenshots), they add language highlighting, formatting and snippets (Snippets are one of the Atom features I’ve just started using) to Atom, in varying degrees:</p>
           <ul class="postList">
            <li name="eb76" id="eb76" class="graf graf--li graf-after--p"><a href="https://atom.io/packages/Atom-Syntax-highlighting-for-Sass" data-href="https://atom.io/packages/Atom-Syntax-highlighting-for-Sass" class="markup--anchor markup--li-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">atom-syntax-highlighting-for-sass</a></li>
            <li name="73f6" id="73f6" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li"><a href="https://atom.io/packages/language-liquid" data-href="https://atom.io/packages/language-liquid" class="markup--anchor markup--li-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">language-liquid</a></li>
            <li name="a9a4" id="a9a4" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li"><a href="https://atom.io/packages/atom-liquid-snippets" data-href="https://atom.io/packages/atom-liquid-snippets" class="markup--anchor markup--li-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">atom-liquid-snippets</a></li>
            <li name="884a" id="884a" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li"><a href="https://atom.io/packages/django-templates" data-href="https://atom.io/packages/django-templates" class="markup--anchor markup--li-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">django-templates</a>?—?I work a lot with Jekyll, and its templates are liquid, which are based on django templates.</li>
            <li name="7dc9" id="7dc9" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li"><a href="https://atom.io/packages/language-swift" data-href="https://atom.io/packages/language-swift" class="markup--anchor markup--li-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">language-swift</a></li>
            <li name="af05" id="af05" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li"><a href="https://atom.io/packages/language-restructuredtext" data-href="https://atom.io/packages/language-restructuredtext" class="markup--anchor markup--li-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">language-restructuredtext</a></li>
            <li name="d061" id="d061" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li"><a href="https://atom.io/packages/language-latex" data-href="https://atom.io/packages/language-latex" class="markup--anchor markup--li-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">language-latex</a></li>
            <li name="61fc" id="61fc" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li"><a href="https://atom.io/packages/language-gradle" data-href="https://atom.io/packages/language-gradle" class="markup--anchor markup--li-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">language-gradle</a></li>
            <li name="2a5a" id="2a5a" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li"><a href="https://atom.io/packages/language-docker" data-href="https://atom.io/packages/language-docker" class="markup--anchor markup--li-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">language-docker</a></li>
            <li name="f284" id="f284" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li"><a href="https://atom.io/packages/linter-swiftc" data-href="https://atom.io/packages/linter-swiftc" class="markup--anchor markup--li-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">linter-swiftc</a></li>
            <li name="e693" id="e693" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li"><a href="https://atom.io/packages/linter-scss-lint" data-href="https://atom.io/packages/linter-scss-lint" class="markup--anchor markup--li-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">linter-scss-lint</a></li>
            <li name="ccc9" id="ccc9" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li"><a href="https://atom.io/packages/linter-jsonlint" data-href="https://atom.io/packages/linter-jsonlint" class="markup--anchor markup--li-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">linter-jsonlint</a></li>
            <li name="ddb2" id="ddb2" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li"><a href="https://atom.io/packages/linter-htmlhint" data-href="https://atom.io/packages/linter-htmlhint" class="markup--anchor markup--li-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">linter-htmlhint</a></li>
            <li name="b770" id="b770" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li"><a href="https://atom.io/packages/linter-javac" data-href="https://atom.io/packages/linter-javac" class="markup--anchor markup--li-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">linter-javac</a></li>
            <li name="683f" id="683f" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li"><a href="https://atom.io/packages/linter-js-yaml" data-href="https://atom.io/packages/linter-js-yaml" class="markup--anchor markup--li-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">linter-js-yaml</a></li>
            <li name="8030" id="8030" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li"><a href="https://atom.io/packages/linter-csslint" data-href="https://atom.io/packages/linter-csslint" class="markup--anchor markup--li-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">linter-csslint</a></li>
            <li name="197a" id="197a" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li"><a href="https://atom.io/packages/linter-jshint" data-href="https://atom.io/packages/linter-jshint" class="markup--anchor markup--li-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">linter-jshint</a></li>
            <li name="2056" id="2056" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li"><a href="https://atom.io/packages/linter-clang" data-href="https://atom.io/packages/linter-clang" class="markup--anchor markup--li-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">linter-clang</a></li>
            <li name="5d93" id="5d93" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li"><a href="https://atom.io/packages/linter-chktex" data-href="https://atom.io/packages/linter-chktex" class="markup--anchor markup--li-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">linter-chktex</a></li>

            <li name="59f1" id="59f1" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li"><a href="https://atom.io/packages/linter-markdown" data-href="https://atom.io/packages/linter-markdown" class="markup--anchor markup--li-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">linter-markdown</a></li>
            <li name="a8dc" id="a8dc" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li"><a href="https://atom.io/packages/linter-package-json-validator" data-href="https://atom.io/packages/linter-package-json-validator" class="markup--anchor markup--li-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">linter-package-json-validator</a></li>
            <li name="f40d" id="f40d" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li"><a href="https://atom.io/packages/linter-shellcheck" data-href="https://atom.io/packages/linter-shellcheck" class="markup--anchor markup--li-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">linter-shellcheck</a></li>
           </ul>
           <h4 name="472b" id="472b" class="graf graf--h4 graf-after--li">Automate yourself</h4>
           <p name="9723" id="9723" class="graf graf--p graf-after--h4">Why waste time repeating yourself when packages can help!</p>
           <p name="fd53" id="fd53" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">The <a href="https://atom.io/packages/autoclose-html" data-href="https://atom.io/packages/autoclose-html" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">autoclose-html</a> package adds closing tags to HTML elements you add into your code or code snippets.</p>
           <p name="8822" id="8822" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p"><a href="https://atom.io/packages/dash" data-href="https://atom.io/packages/dash" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Atom Dash</a> adds Atom support for <a href="https://kapeli.com/dash" data-href="https://kapeli.com/dash" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Dash</a>, the ever so helpful offline documentation browser.</p>
           <p name="35e0" id="35e0" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">I use occasionally use <a href="https://github.com/hakimel/reveal.js/" data-href="https://github.com/hakimel/reveal.js/" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">RevealJS</a> for presentations and <a href="https://atom.io/packages/grunt-runner" data-href="https://atom.io/packages/grunt-runner" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Grunt Runner</a> for running <a href="http://gruntjs.com/" data-href="http://gruntjs.com/" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Grunt tasks</a> let’s me start presentations from inside Atom.</p>
           <p name="31f7" id="31f7" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">The <a href="https://atom.io/packages/jekyll" data-href="https://atom.io/packages/jekyll" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Jekyll</a> package is a comprehensive package that adds Jekyll snippets, shortcut methods, grammars, server management and is configuration aware (of the contents of your Jekyll <em class="markup--em markup--p-em">config.yml</em> file). I should use this package more, but it frequently doesn’t work and isn’t very verbose ?.</p>
           <p name="703e" id="703e" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">Using <a href="https://atom.io/packages/color-picker" data-href="https://atom.io/packages/color-picker" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Color Picker</a> you can summon a pop-up colour picker inline in your files.</p>
           <figure name="e7fa" id="e7fa" class="graf graf--figure graf--iframe graf-after--p">
            <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder is-locked">
             <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder-fill" style="padding-bottom: 56.2%;"></div>
             <div class="iframeContainer">
              <iframe data-width="854" data-height="480" width="700" height="393" src="/media/3b8719ad782bfddcc357c97a0ced83eb?postId=e7a89969a876" data-media-id="3b8719ad782bfddcc357c97a0ced83eb" allowfullscreen frameborder="0"></iframe>
             </div>
            </div>
           </figure>
           <h4 name="7369" id="7369" class="graf graf--h4 graf-after--figure">Project Management</h4>
           <p name="66e2" id="66e2" class="graf graf--p graf-after--h4"><a href="https://atom.io/packages/project-manager" data-href="https://atom.io/packages/project-manager" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Project Manager</a> allows you to set folders as projects and then open and switch between them.</p>
           <figure name="aee4" id="aee4" class="graf graf--figure graf--iframe graf-after--p">
            <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder is-locked">
             <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder-fill" style="padding-bottom: 56.2%;"></div>
             <div class="iframeContainer">
              <iframe data-width="854" data-height="480" width="700" height="393" src="/media/2f66e5f42c9d113d255dbd012a349811?postId=e7a89969a876" data-media-id="2f66e5f42c9d113d255dbd012a349811" allowfullscreen frameborder="0"></iframe>
             </div>
            </div>
           </figure>
           <p name="bd7d" id="bd7d" class="graf graf--p graf-after--figure">If you can’t remember the name of a file or the correct path to it, <a href="https://atom.io/packages/autocomplete-paths" data-href="https://atom.io/packages/autocomplete-paths" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">autocomplete-paths</a> will help. Sometimes it can be too keen, requiring judicious use of the <em class="markup--em markup--p-em">esc</em> key to stop inserting file names all over your document.</p>
           <figure name="04a4" id="04a4" class="graf graf--figure graf--iframe graf-after--p">
            <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder is-locked">
             <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder-fill" style="padding-bottom: 75%;"></div>
             <div class="iframeContainer">
              <iframe data-width="640" data-height="480" width="640" height="480" src="/media/a2caa8adfc9f290e5020594afe2e97d7?postId=e7a89969a876" data-media-id="a2caa8adfc9f290e5020594afe2e97d7" allowfullscreen frameborder="0"></iframe>
             </div>
            </div>
           </figure>
           <p name="96f8" id="96f8" class="graf graf--p graf-after--figure">Make your project view look nicer with colourful file type icons from <a href="https://atom.io/packages/file-icons" data-href="https://atom.io/packages/file-icons" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">file-icons</a>. The Unity UI theme hides these, so make sure you show them by checking the <em class="markup--em markup--p-em">Force Show</em> setting in the package settings.</p>
           <h4 name="a6bc" id="a6bc" class="graf graf--h4 graf-after--p">Collaboration</h4>
           <p name="63c0" id="63c0" class="graf graf--p graf-after--h4"><a href="https://atom.io/packages/git-time-machine" data-href="https://atom.io/packages/git-time-machine" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">git-time-machine</a> is a great package that lets you browse and compare git history for a file in Atom.</p>
           <figure name="3d5d" id="3d5d" class="graf graf--figure graf--iframe graf-after--p">
            <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder is-locked">
             <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder-fill" style="padding-bottom: 75%;"></div>
             <div class="iframeContainer">
              <iframe data-width="640" data-height="480" width="640" height="480" src="/media/887cd79196d4e4765cc7a949ba2d49e2?postId=e7a89969a876" data-media-id="887cd79196d4e4765cc7a949ba2d49e2" allowfullscreen frameborder="0"></iframe>
             </div>
            </div>
           </figure>
           <p name="02cd" id="02cd" class="graf graf--p graf-after--figure">The <a href="https://atom.io/packages/pull-requests" data-href="https://atom.io/packages/pull-requests" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Pull requests</a> package is super cool, allowing you to view comments on pull requests inline in your file. It occasionally times out on network connections and I had issues with private / business repositories, but it usually catches up.</p>
           <figure name="42e4" id="42e4" class="graf graf--figure graf--iframe graf-after--p">
            <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder is-locked">
             <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder-fill" style="padding-bottom: 56.2%;"></div>
             <div class="iframeContainer">
              <iframe data-width="854" data-height="480" width="700" height="393" src="/media/5f93cca1cbd4077de8a171cba8e6b728?postId=e7a89969a876" data-media-id="5f93cca1cbd4077de8a171cba8e6b728" allowfullscreen frameborder="0"></iframe>
             </div>
            </div>
           </figure>
           <h4 name="d16b" id="d16b" class="graf graf--h4 graf-after--figure">Write Better</h4>
           <p name="ddbf" id="ddbf" class="graf graf--p graf-after--h4">OK, this is what you’re really interested in ?.</p>
           <p name="5026" id="5026" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">I have been using <a href="https://atom.io/packages/linter-write-good" data-href="https://atom.io/packages/linter-write-good" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">linter-write-good</a> for some time and have found it useful. It offers suggestions to make your writing better based on the <a href="https://github.com/btford/write-good" data-href="https://github.com/btford/write-good" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">NPM write-good module</a>. It wont always be right or relevant, but it has helped me a lot.</p>
           <figure name="7be1" id="7be1" class="graf graf--figure graf--iframe graf-after--p">
            <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder is-locked">
             <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder-fill" style="padding-bottom: 56.2%;"></div>
             <div class="iframeContainer">
              <iframe data-width="854" data-height="480" width="700" height="393" src="/media/df732390601ce45f6559a0bded452bda?postId=e7a89969a876" data-media-id="df732390601ce45f6559a0bded452bda" allowfullscreen frameborder="0"></iframe>
             </div>
            </div>
           </figure>
           <p name="0716" id="0716" class="graf graf--p graf-after--figure">I am still undecided on <a href="https://atom.io/packages/linter-alex" data-href="https://atom.io/packages/linter-alex" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Alex Linter</a>, it uses <a href="http://alexjs.com/" data-href="http://alexjs.com/" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">AlexJS</a> to catch inconsiderate writing. I have found it overly sensitive, highlighting words like Australian and American as ‘potentially profane’, which is odd. It will also highlight words with double meanings, such as ‘shoot a photo’. I’m still assessing how useful it is to me.</p>
           <figure name="a927" id="a927" class="graf graf--figure graf--iframe graf-after--p">
            <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder is-locked">
             <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder-fill" style="padding-bottom: 56.2%;"></div>
             <div class="iframeContainer">
              <iframe data-width="854" data-height="480" width="700" height="393" src="/media/28ff5a7b95015e2e7b1114a0181feda6?postId=e7a89969a876" data-media-id="28ff5a7b95015e2e7b1114a0181feda6" allowfullscreen frameborder="0"></iframe>
             </div>
            </div>
           </figure>
           <p name="64a2" id="64a2" class="graf graf--p graf-after--figure">The <a href="https://atom.io/packages/linter-just-say-no" data-href="https://atom.io/packages/linter-just-say-no" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Just Say No</a> linter highlights ‘<a href="http://theeditorsblog.net/2010/11/18/hedge-words/" data-href="http://theeditorsblog.net/2010/11/18/hedge-words/" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">hedge words</a>’. It’s functionality crosses over slightly with the Write Good linter, but I still find it useful.</p>
           <p name="3f89" id="3f89" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">I replaced the inbuilt spell checker in Atom, because the <a href="https://atom.io/packages/linter-spell" data-href="https://atom.io/packages/linter-spell" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Spell Linter</a> allows you to select dictionaries (You can switch between UK and US English ?), add custom words (great for tech jargon), and it has a nicer interface. You will need a lspell compatible dictionary installed (I installed <a href="http://aspell.net/" data-href="http://aspell.net/" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Aspell</a> with Homebrew) and the <a href="https://atom.io/packages/intentions" data-href="https://atom.io/packages/intentions" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">intentions</a> package which adds a nice pop-up over issues that I wish other packages would use.</p>
           <figure name="288d" id="288d" class="graf graf--figure graf--iframe graf-after--p">
            <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder is-locked">
             <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder-fill" style="padding-bottom: 75%;"></div>
             <div class="iframeContainer">
              <iframe data-width="640" data-height="480" width="640" height="480" src="/media/c298647842b8c333972ff64b844641c6?postId=e7a89969a876" data-media-id="c298647842b8c333972ff64b844641c6" allowfullscreen frameborder="0"></iframe>
             </div>
            </div>
           </figure>
           <p name="ef25" id="ef25" class="graf graf--p graf-after--figure"><a href="https://atom.io/packages/typewriter" data-href="https://atom.io/packages/typewriter" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Typewriter</a> “improves your writing experience” by centring the layout removing scroll-bars (unless you scroll) and other tweaks. I’m not 100% on this package, as sometimes (and this may be package conflicts) it creates unnecessary horizontal scrolling and I end up with a lot of white space, which I know is kind of the point of the package, but I’m not a big fan of it ?.</p>
           <p name="814c" id="814c" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">The <a href="https://atom.io/packages/wordcount" data-href="https://atom.io/packages/wordcount" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Wordcount</a> package counts words and characters. Simple.</p>
           <p name="4fe0" id="4fe0" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p"><a href="https://atom.io/packages/markdown-writer" data-href="https://atom.io/packages/markdown-writer" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Markdown Writer</a> provides a set of shortcuts and functions for making working with Markdown easier. It also works well with static site generators that use Markdown for posts.</p>
           <p name="dee4" id="dee4" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">I love <a href="http://pandoc.org/getting-started.html" data-href="http://pandoc.org/getting-started.html" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Pandoc</a>, and with the <a href="https://atom.io/packages/pandoc-convert" data-href="https://atom.io/packages/pandoc-convert" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Pandoc convert</a> and <a href="https://atom.io/packages/pandoc" data-href="https://atom.io/packages/pandoc" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Pandoc previewer</a> packages I can utilise Pandoc for previewing and exporting documents in the vast amount of options it offers.</p>
           <p name="e38d" id="e38d" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">It can be jumpy, but <a href="https://atom.io/packages/markdown-scroll-sync" data-href="https://atom.io/packages/markdown-scroll-sync" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Markdown scroll sync</a> keeps your source and preview markdown in sync with each other.</p>
           <h4 name="44d8" id="44d8" class="graf graf--h4 graf-after--p">Packages from&nbsp;Me</h4>
           <p name="b095" id="b095" class="graf graf--p graf-after--h4">If you like writing in Markdown, but also use Medium, then my <a href="https://atom.io/packages/medium-export" data-href="https://atom.io/packages/medium-export" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Medium Export</a> lets you export straight to your Medium drafts. It needs work, but functions fine.</p>
           <p name="0187" id="0187" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">I am also working (slowly) on the ‘Editors friend’ package that sets configurable lists of search/replace strings to help reduce the amount of repetitive editing you do.</p>
           <h4 name="cbc3" id="cbc3" class="graf graf--h4 graf-after--p">What’s in your&nbsp;Atom?</h4>
           <p name="fac3" id="fac3" class="graf graf--p graf-after--h4">And that’s me! I love the extensibility of Atom and would welcome your comments on how you’ve set it up for your needs.</p>
           <blockquote name="0208" id="0208" class="graf graf--blockquote graf-after--p">
            <a href="http://bit.ly/Hackernoon" data-href="http://bit.ly/Hackernoon" class="markup--anchor markup--blockquote-anchor" rel="noopener nofollow noopener" target="_blank">Hacker Noon</a> is how hackers start their afternoons. We’re a part of the 
            <a href="http://bit.ly/atAMIatAMI" data-href="http://bit.ly/atAMIatAMI" class="markup--anchor markup--blockquote-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener nofollow noopener" target="_blank">@AMI</a>family. We are now 
            <a href="http://bit.ly/hackernoonsubmission" data-href="http://bit.ly/hackernoonsubmission" class="markup--anchor markup--blockquote-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener nofollow noopener" target="_blank">accepting submissions</a> and happy to 
            <a href="mailto:partners@amipublications.com" data-href="mailto:partners@amipublications.com" class="markup--anchor markup--blockquote-anchor" target="_blank">discuss advertising &amp;sponsorship</a> opportunities.
           </blockquote>

            <a href="https://goo.gl/4ofytp" data-href="https://goo.gl/4ofytp" class="markup--anchor markup--blockquote-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">read our about page</a>, 
            <a href="http://bit.ly/HackernoonFB" data-href="http://bit.ly/HackernoonFB" class="markup--anchor markup--blockquote-anchor" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">like/message us on Facebook</a>, or simply,
